			NULL, "\"......사토코?", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s14/06/210600657", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　どうしたの、沙都子っ？！」",
			NULL, "왜 그래요, 사토코?!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//r詩音の緊迫した悲鳴が響き渡って、私ははっと我に返る。見ると沙都子は詩音の腕の中で頭を抱えたまま、がたがたと震えながらうわ言のように呟きを繰り返し、うつろな目で何度も何度も首を振っていた。
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLineAll("", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine(NULL, "", NULL, "<size=-2>", Line_Continue); }
	OutputLine(NULL, "詩音の緊迫した悲鳴が響き渡って、私ははっと我に返る。見ると沙都子は詩音の腕の中で頭を抱えたまま、がたがたと震えながらうわ言のように呟きを繰り返し、うつろな目で何度も何度も首を振っていた。",
			NULL, "시온의 절박한 비명소리에 정신이 번쩍 들어 돌아보니, 시온의 품 안에 안긴 사토코가 머리를 움켜쥔 채, 공허한 눈으로 헛소리를 중얼거리며 바들바들 떨면서 고개를 흔들고 있었다.", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	ModDrawCharacter(3, 4, "sprite/sa2a_sakebu_a1_", "0", 160, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 20, 200, TRUE );

//沙都子rvS14/04/210400302.「…ち、違う……！kvS14/04/210400303.　私じゃない…！kvS14/04/210400304.　私は、なにも…なにもっ…！！」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#fcdb77>沙都子</color>", NULL, "<color=#fcdb77>사토코</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 4, "ps3/s14/04/210400302", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「…ち、違う……！",
			NULL, "\"...아, 아니야......!", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 4, "ps3/s14/04/210400303", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　私じゃない…！",
			NULL, "내가 아니야...!", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 4, "ps3/s14/04/210400304", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　私は、なにも…なにもっ…！！」",
			NULL, "나는, 아무... 아무것도...!!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

//梨花rvS14/05/210500843.「沙都子っ！！」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#6972c1>梨花</color>", NULL, "<color=#6972c1>리카</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 5, "ps3/s14/05/210500843", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「沙都子っ！！」",
			NULL, "\"사토코!!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	ModDrawCharacter(5, 6, "sprite/si1a_ikari_a1_", "0", -160, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 18, 200, TRUE );

//詩音rvS14/06/210600658.「沙都子、しっかりして……沙都子ぉっ！！」
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>시온</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s14/06/210600658", 256, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「沙都子、しっかりして……沙都子ぉっ！！」",
			NULL, "\"사토코, 정신 차려요...... 사토코!!\"", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DisableWindow();
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 3000 );
	DrawBustshotWithFiltering(6, "cinema", "x", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 1300, TRUE );
	DrawBustshot(7, "title02", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 26, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 2000 );
	DrawBustshot(6, "black", 0, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 25, 3000, TRUE );
	Wait( 1000 );
	FadeBustshotWithFiltering( 7, "x", 1, FALSE, 0, 0, 1000, TRUE );
	DrawScene( "black", 3000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );

	DrawSceneWithMask("tips/omot003", "mask_1900", 7, 0, 300 );
	SetValidityOfInput( FALSE );
	Wait( 5000 );
	SetValidityOfInput( TRUE );
	DrawSceneWithMask("black", "mask_1900", 7, 0, 300 );
